  <script id="/templates/cta/learning-path-gifting-global-module.html" type="text/ng-template">
   <script>
var $rootScope = angular.element(document.body).injector().get('$rootScope');
var userLoggedIn = false;
addGift();
$rootScope.$on('user:login', function() {
  userLoggedIn = true;
  addGift();
});
function addGift() {
  // console.log('addGift');
  try {
    var $templateCache = angular.element(document.body).injector().get('$templateCache');
    var hasGiftTemplate = $templateCache.get('/cta-gift-header.html');
    var $learningPath = angular.element(document.querySelector('.learning-path-page-header'));
    var learningPath = $learningPath && $learningPath.scope() && $learningPath.scope().$parent && $learningPath.scope().$parent.learningPath;
    var productCard = document.querySelector('.learning-path-product-card');
    var priceBlock = document.querySelector('.price-block + div');
    if (!hasGiftTemplate || !learningPath || (!learningPath.statesReady && !userLoggedIn) || !priceBlock || !productCard) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        addGift();
      }, 500);
      return;
    }
    var $compile = angular.element(document.body).injector().get('$compile');
    var attach = productCard;
    if (!learningPath.hasAccessRights && learningPath.current_price && learningPath.flagged.for_sale && !userLoggedIn) {
      attach = priceBlock;
    }
    // console.log(learningPath, attach);
    var $attach = angular.element(attach);
    var $templateScope = $learningPath.scope().$new(false);
    var $template = angular.element('<div><div class="text-center" login-required via="gift" ng-if="learningPath.product" ng-init="giftProductId = {_id: learningPath.product}"><cta-gift product="giftProductId" cl-cta-gift-template="/cta-gift-header.html"></cta-gift></div></div>');
    $compile($template)($templateScope);
    $attach.append($template);
  } catch (giftingError) {
    console.log('Error adding gifting cta.', giftingError);
  }
}
  </script>
  <script id="/cta-gift-header.html" type="text/ng-template">
   <a href class="gift-link text-uppercase block-level margin-top-l font-size-s font-weight-bold text-nowrap" data-cta="gift" ng-click="$event.preventDefault();startGifting()">
  <i class="fa fa-gift"></i>
  Give as a gift
</a>
  </script>

        <script>
         //Play video in big player

$(document).on('click','#bigPlayer2Play',function(){
	$("#bigPlayer2Play").hide();
	$(".big-video2 h4").html("How to Find Yourself");
	//setTimeout(function(){
	//	$(".cllp-classes-module .button-container").show();
	//	$("#bigVideo2PlayButton").hide();
	//	$("#bigVideo2PauseButton").show();
	//},35000); //35 seconds
});

var pbnc=0;

$(document).on('click','.big-video2-title',function(){
	if($(this).text()=="How to Find Yourself"&&pbnc==0) {
		$("#bigPlayer2Play").click();
		pbnc++;
	}
});

$(document).on('click','#bigVideo2PauseButton',function(){
	$(this).hide();
	$("#pauseVideo2Action").click();
	$("#bigVideo2PlayButton").show();
});

$(document).on('click','#bigVideo2PlayButton',function(){
	$(this).hide();
	$("#playVideo2Action").click();
	$("#bigVideo2PauseButton").show();
});


//Carousel thumbnails click function
var prev_player="";
var seemoretimeout;

$("#videoPlayerGroup1 .classes-carousel .slide").click(function(){

	//clearTimeout(seemoretimeout);

	var clicked_element = $(this).closest(".slide");
	
	
	if ($(window).width() < 768) {
		if(clicked_element.attr("data-clicked")!="true") {
			var vc=$(this).find('.image-container');
			vc.html("");
			
			$(".cl-video2-player").appendTo(vc);
			clicked_element.attr("data-clicked","true");
		}
				
		
		if(prev_player!="" && !prev_player.is(clicked_element)) {
			prev_player.attr("data-clicked","false");
			prev_player.find(".image-container").html(prev_player.find(".image-container").attr("data-html"));
		}
		
		prev_player=clicked_element;
					
	}
	

	$(".big-video2 .button-container, #bigPlayer2Play, .cllp-classes-module .button-container").hide();
	
	$(".big-video2 .btn").attr('href',clicked_element.attr('data-html'));
	$(".big-video2 h4").text(clicked_element.find('h4').text());
	$(".big-video2 .big-video2-author").text(clicked_element.find('.video2-author').text());
	$(".big-video2 .big-video2-students").text(clicked_element.find('.video2-students').text());
	$(".big-video2 .big-video2-Lessons").text(clicked_element.find('.video2-Lessons').text());
	$(".big-video2 .channel2").text(clicked_element.find('.channel2').text());
	
	//seemoretimeout = setTimeout(function(){
	//	$(".cllp-classes-module .button-container").show();
	//	$("#bigVideo2PlayButton").hide();
	//	$("#bigVideo2PauseButton").show();
	//},35000); //35 seconds
});
        </script>

         //Window load tweaks
(function hideSeeTheClass(){
	//if($(".cllp-classes-module .button-container").length) {
	//	$(".cllp-classes-module .button-container").hide();
		
		if ($(window).width() < 768) {
			$(".cllp-classes-module .image-container").each(function() {
				$(this).attr("data-html",$(this).html());
			});
		}
		
	//} else {
	//	setTimeout(function(){
	//		hideSeeTheClass();
	//	},1000); //try again in a second		
	//}
})();

function adjustArrows(){
	//adjust position of the carousel arrows
	var h=$(".cllp-classes-module .image-container").height()/2+$(".cllp-classes-module a .channel").outerHeight(true);
	$(".cllp-classes-module .slick-prev, .cllp-classes-module .slick-next").css('top',h-12);
	
	var h2=$(".student-carousel .image-container").height()/2;
	$(".gray-bg-students .slick-prev, .gray-bg-students .slick-next").css('top',h2-12);
}

(function carouselImagesLoaded(){
	if($(".cllp-classes-module .classes-carousel img").first().height()>35 && $(".student-carousel .image-container").first().height()>35) {
		adjustArrows();
	} else {
		setTimeout(function(){
			carouselImagesLoaded();
		},1000); //try again in a second
	}

})();

(function adjustCarouselTitleHeight(){
	setTimeout(function(){
		var maxHeight = Math.max.apply(null, $(".cllp-classes-module .slide h4").map(function ()
		{
			return $(this).height();
		}).get());
		
		$(".cllp-classes-module .slide h4").css('min-height',maxHeight);
	},1000);
	
})();

var resizetimeout;
$(window).on('resize',function(){
  clearTimeout(resizetimeout);
  resize = setTimeout(adjustArrows, 100);
});

//Play video in big player

$(document).on('click','#bigPlayerPlay',function(){
	$("#bigPlayerPlay").hide();
	$(".big-video h4").html("<a href='https://www.creativelive.com/class/how-to-launch-a-photography-business-pye-jirsa'>How to Start a Photography Business</a>");
	//setTimeout(function(){
	//	$(".cllp-classes-module .button-container").show();
	//	$("#bigVideoPlayButton").hide();
	//	$("#bigVideoPauseButton").show();
	//},35000); //35 seconds
});

var pbnc=0;

$(document).on('click','.big-video-title',function(){
	if($(this).text()=="How to Start a Photography Business"&&pbnc==0) {
		$("#bigPlayerPlay").click();
		pbnc++;
	}
});

$(document).on('click','#bigVideoPauseButton',function(){
	$(this).hide();
	$("#pauseVideoAction").click();
	$("#bigVideoPlayButton").show();
});

$(document).on('click','#bigVideoPlayButton',function(){
	$(this).hide();
	$("#playVideoAction").click();
	$("#bigVideoPauseButton").show();
});


//Carousel thumbnails click function
var prev_player="";
var seemoretimeout;

$(".classes-carousel .slide").click(function(){

	//clearTimeout(seemoretimeout);

	var clicked_element = $(this).closest(".slide");
	
	
	if ($(window).width() < 768) {
		if(clicked_element.attr("data-clicked")!="true") {
			var vc=$(this).find('.image-container');
			vc.html("");
			
			$(".cl-video-player").appendTo(vc);
			clicked_element.attr("data-clicked","true");
		}
				
		
		if(prev_player!="" && !prev_player.is(clicked_element)) {
			prev_player.attr("data-clicked","false");
			prev_player.find(".image-container").html(prev_player.find(".image-container").attr("data-html"));
		}
		
		prev_player=clicked_element;
					
	}
	

	$(".big-video .button-container, #bigPlayerPlay, .cllp-classes-module .button-container").hide();
	
	$(".big-video .btn").attr('href',clicked_element.attr('data-html'));
	$(".big-video h4").html("<a href='"+clicked_element.attr('data-link')+"'>"+clicked_element.find('h4').text()+"</a>");
	$(".big-video .big-video-author").text(clicked_element.find('.video-author').text());
	$(".big-video .big-video-students").text(clicked_element.find('.video-students').text());
	$(".big-video .big-video-Lessons").text(clicked_element.find('.video-Lessons').text());
	$(".big-video .channel").text(clicked_element.find('.channel').text());
	
	//seemoretimeout = setTimeout(function(){
	//	$(".cllp-classes-module .button-container").show();
	//	$("#bigVideoPlayButton").hide();
	//	$("#bigVideoPauseButton").show();
	//},35000); //35 seconds
});


//Fading images carousel

(function slideLoop(){
	//duration of each slide
	var pause_time=2500;

	$("#text5").show();
	//fade to slide 4
	$("#line-text").text("youre full time with your creativity.").fadeIn(500);
	$("#slide5").fadeOut(500, function(){
		
		setTimeout(function(){
			//fade to slide 3
			$("#line-text").text("your favorite color is graphite.").fadeIn(500);
			$("#slide4").fadeOut(500, function(){
			
			setTimeout(function(){	
				//fade to slide 2
				$("#line-text").text("youre addicted to pretty paper.").fadeIn(500);
				$("#slide3").fadeOut(500, function(){
				
				setTimeout(function(){
					//fade to slide 1
					$("#line-text").text("you love pulling all-nighters.").fadeIn(500);
					$("#slide2").fadeOut(500, function(){
					
					setTimeout(function(){	
						//fade to slide 5
						$("#line-text").text("you spend lunch with your Canon.").fadeIn(500);
						$("#slide5").fadeIn(500, function(){
						
						setTimeout(function(){
							//display all slides behind slide 5
							$("#slide1, #slide2, #slide3, #slide4").show();	
							//start over
							slideLoop();
						},pause_time);
						});
					},pause_time);
					});					
				},pause_time);
				});
			},pause_time);
			});
		},pause_time);
	});
})();
	
//Slick Slider init 

(function initSlick(){
	
	if((typeof $.fn.slick !== 'undefined')) {
		//init sliders
		$('.classes-carousel').slick({
		  infinite: false,
		  slidesToShow: 4,
		  slidesToScroll: 4,
		  dots: false,
		  responsive: [
			{
			  breakpoint: 1200,
			  settings: {
				slidesToShow: 3,
				slidesToScroll: 3
			  }
			},
			{
			  breakpoint: 992,
			  settings: {
				slidesToShow: 2,
				slidesToScroll: 2
			  }
			},
			{
			  breakpoint: 768,
			  settings: {
				slidesToShow: 1,
				slidesToScroll: 1
			  }
			}
		  ]
		});
		
		$('.student-carousel').slick({
		  infinite: false,
		  slidesToShow: 3,
		  slidesToScroll: 3,
		  dots: false,
		  responsive: [
			{
			  breakpoint: 992,
			  settings: {
				slidesToShow: 2,
				slidesToScroll: 2
			  }
			},
			{
			  breakpoint: 768,
			  settings: {
				slidesToShow: 1,
				slidesToScroll: 1,
				variableWidth: false
			  }
			}
		  ]
		});
	
	} else { //try again in a second
		setTimeout(function(){initSlick();},1000);
	}
})();
